# K-05 Codex Security Review ? Phase 3.1 hotfix-3
# Focus: DB migration + 4 new RPCs + 5 new server actions + asset_index trust boundary

## Context

YAGI Workshop is a Next.js 15 + Supabase + TypeScript application.
Phase 3.1 hotfix-3 adds:
- 2 new jsonb columns on `project_boards` (attached_pdfs, attached_urls)
- 4 SECURITY DEFINER RPCs in PostgreSQL
- Extended seed RPC
- 5 new server actions in board-actions.ts
- AttachmentsSection client component with URL validation
- LockButton / LockedBanner components for yagi_admin role gate
- Lock state cascade enforcement

Primary reviewer question: Are there any security vulnerabilities in the new code?

---

## Focus Area 1: New RPC Privilege Escalation + Role Check + Lock Bypass + search_path

File: `supabase/migrations/20260429144523_phase_3_1_hotfix_3_attachments.sql`

RPCs to review:
1. `add_project_board_pdf(p_board_id uuid, p_storage_key text, p_filename text, p_size_bytes bigint)`
2. `add_project_board_url(p_board_id uuid, p_url text, p_title text, p_thumbnail_url text, p_provider text, p_note text)`
3. `remove_project_board_attachment(p_board_id uuid, p_kind text, p_attachment_id uuid)`
4. `update_project_board_url_note(p_board_id uuid, p_attachment_id uuid, p_note text)`

Questions:
- Does each RPC correctly verify the caller is either the board's project owner OR yagi_admin?
- Is the `is_locked` check correctly applied? Can a non-admin client bypass lock by calling the RPC directly?
- Is `SET search_path = public, pg_temp` correctly set on all 4? Does this prevent search_path injection?
- Does `jsonb_build_object` usage prevent SQL injection via jsonb construction?
- Are UUID values for attachment IDs generated server-side (non-predictable)?
- Is the `p_storage_key` prefix validation enforced (`project-wizard/` or `project-board/<board_id>/`, no `..`, no absolute paths)?

---

## Focus Area 2: Extended Seed RPC Backward Compat + Safe Defaults

RPC: `seed_project_board_from_wizard` (5-arg version)

Questions:
- Does the 5-arg version with `DEFAULT '[]'::jsonb` preserve backward compat with 3-arg callers?
- Can a caller supply malicious content in `p_initial_attached_pdfs` or `p_initial_attached_urls`?
- Is the `search_path` correctly set?

---

## Focus Area 3: RLS on New Columns ? Cross-Tenant Leak via Attachment ID Guessing

Questions:
- Do the SELECT/UPDATE policies on `project_boards` correctly cover `attached_pdfs` and `attached_urls`?
- Can user A guess a UUID attachment ID belonging to user B and remove/update it via RPC?
- The RPC verifies ownership via `project_boards.project_id -> projects.created_by` ? is this join correct and complete?

---

## Focus Area 4: Server Actions Trust Boundary ? Client Never Supplies asset_index

File: `src/app/[locale]/app/projects/[id]/board-actions.ts`

5 new actions: addPdfAttachmentAction, removePdfAttachmentAction, addUrlAttachmentAction, updateUrlNoteAction, removeUrlAttachmentAction

Questions:
- Does each action verify user session before proceeding?
- Does each action call `recomputeAndUpdateAssetIndex` server-side after RPC (never trusting client-supplied asset_index)?
- In `addPdfAttachmentAction`: is the storage key generated server-side (not client-supplied)?
- In `addUrlAttachmentAction`: is the URL validated server-side (only http/https) BEFORE calling RPC?

---

## Focus Area 5: extractAssetIndex Dedup Correctness

File: `src/lib/board/asset-index.ts`

Questions:
- When the same URL appears in both canvas url-card shapes AND attached_urls, is deduplication correct?
- Does the `duplicate:true` flag correctly mark the canvas entry (not the attached entry)?
- Is sort order deterministic (attached before canvas, ascending added_at within each group)?

---

## Focus Area 6: toggle_project_board_lock yagi_admin-Only at BOTH Layers

File: `board-actions.ts` ? `toggleBoardLockAction`

Questions:
- Does the action check `user_roles` for `yagi_admin` before calling RPC?
- Does the RPC also enforce `yagi_admin` (defense-in-depth)?
- Can a non-admin user call `toggleBoardLockAction` directly and succeed?

---

## Focus Area 7: URL Validation ? Client + Server + RPC

Client: `attachments-section.tsx` ? `isValidUrl()` and `BLOCKED_SCHEMES`
Server: `board-actions.ts` ? `validateUrlScheme()`
RPC: `add_project_board_url` ? provider/url validation

Questions:
- Does client validation reject `javascript:`, `data:`, `file:`, `chrome:`, `blob:`, `vbscript:`?
- Does server validation in `validateUrlScheme()` reject non-http/https?
- If client validation is bypassed (raw fetch), does server action still catch it?
- Are there any URL encoding tricks (e.g., `JAVASCRIPT:`, `java\tscript:`) that could bypass checks?

---

In `add_project_board_pdf` RPC:
- Is `p_storage_key` validated to start with `project-wizard/` or `project-board/<board_id>/`?
- Are path traversal attacks (e.g., `project-board/abc/../../../etc/passwd`) rejected?
- Is `..` explicitly rejected?

- Is there a TOCTOU (time-of-check-time-of-use) window between the action's session check and the RPC's lock check?

Questions:

- Does the server independently enforce auth/lock regardless of client reporting?

Questions:

/**
 * asset-index.ts
 * Phase 3.1 hotfix-3 ??Unified asset index normalizer merging three attachment sources:
 *   1. Canvas shapes (yagi-image, yagi-pdf, yagi-url-card) from tldraw snapshot
 *   2. attached_pdfs jsonb column entries
 *   3. attached_urls jsonb column entries
 *
 * Trust boundary: server actions ALWAYS recompute asset_index server-side.
 * Client NEVER supplies asset_index (K-05 + L-041).
 *
 * Pure function ??no I/O, no side effects, easily unit-testable.
 */

// ============================================================
// Attachment types (mirrors DB jsonb shape contracts)
// ============================================================

export type PdfAttachment = {
  id: string;
  storage_key: string;
  filename: string;
  size_bytes: number;
  uploaded_at: string; // ISO string
  uploaded_by: string; // profile_id
};

export type UrlAttachment = {
  id: string;
  url: string;
  title: string | null;
  thumbnail_url: string | null;
  provider: "youtube" | "vimeo" | "generic";
  note: string | null;
  added_at: string; // ISO string
  added_by: string; // profile_id
};

// ============================================================
// Unified asset index entry
// ============================================================

export type AssetIndexEntry = {
  id: string;
  source: "canvas" | "attached_pdf" | "attached_url";
  kind: "image" | "pdf" | "url";
  // Common
  url: string; // for canvas: R2 public URL; for url-attachment: the URL itself; for pdf-attachment: storage_key
  title: string | null;
  thumbnail_url: string | null;
  // Canvas-only
  shape_id?: string;
  // PDF-only
  filename?: string;
  size_bytes?: number;
  // URL-only (attached or canvas url-card)
  provider?: "youtube" | "vimeo" | "generic";
  // Memo (URL-attachment) or caption (canvas image-shape)
  note: string | null;
  added_at: string; // ISO string
  // Set when same URL appears in both canvas url-card shapes AND attached_urls
  duplicate?: boolean;
};

// ============================================================
// extractAssetIndex
// Merges canvas shapes + attached_pdfs + attached_urls into a unified
// flat AssetIndexEntry[].
//
// Sort order: attached items first (source !== 'canvas'), then canvas items,
// within each group sorted by added_at ascending.
//
// Deduplication: if the same URL exists in both canvas url-card shapes AND
// attached_urls, keep both entries ??mark the canvas entry with duplicate:true
// (the attached_url entry has the explicit note and is preferred for display).
//
// Default params preserve backward compat with Phase 3.1 callers that only
// pass the document argument.
// ============================================================

export function extractAssetIndex(
  document: Record<string, unknown> | null | undefined,
  attached_pdfs: PdfAttachment[] = [],
  attached_urls: UrlAttachment[] = []
): AssetIndexEntry[] {
  const canvasEntries: AssetIndexEntry[] = [];
  const attachedEntries: AssetIndexEntry[] = [];

  // --- Build set of URLs in attached_urls for dedup check ---
  const attachedUrlSet = new Set<string>(
    attached_urls.map((u) => u.url.toLowerCase().trim())
  );

  // --- Extract canvas shapes ---
  if (document && typeof document === "object") {
    const store = document.store as Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
    if (store && typeof store === "object") {
      for (const [key, record] of Object.entries(store)) {
        if (!key.startsWith("shape:")) continue;
        if (typeof record !== "object" || record === null) continue;

        const shape = record as {
          type?: string;
          id?: string;
          props?: Record<string, unknown>;
          meta?: Record<string, unknown>;
        };

        if (!shape.type || !shape.props) continue;

        const addedAt =
          typeof shape.meta?.createdAt === "string"
            ? shape.meta.createdAt
            : typeof shape.meta?.addedAt === "string"
              ? shape.meta.addedAt
              : new Date(0).toISOString();

        switch (shape.type) {
          case "yagi-image": {
            const src = shape.props.src as string | undefined;
            if (src) {
              canvasEntries.push({
                id: shape.id ?? key,
                source: "canvas",
                kind: "image",
                url: src,
                title: (shape.props.alt as string) || null,
                thumbnail_url: null,
                shape_id: shape.id ?? key,
                note: null,
                added_at: addedAt,
              });
            }
            break;
          }
          case "yagi-pdf": {
            const src = shape.props.src as string | undefined;
            const filename = shape.props.filename as string | undefined;
            if (src) {
              canvasEntries.push({
                id: shape.id ?? key,
                source: "canvas",
                kind: "pdf",
                url: src,
                title: filename ?? null,
                thumbnail_url: null,
                shape_id: shape.id ?? key,
                filename,
                note: null,
                added_at: addedAt,
              });
            }
            break;
          }
          case "yagi-url-card": {
            const src = shape.props.url as string | undefined;
            const title = shape.props.title as string | undefined;
            const domain = shape.props.domain as string | undefined;
            if (src) {
              const isDuplicate = attachedUrlSet.has(
                src.toLowerCase().trim()
              );
              canvasEntries.push({
                id: shape.id ?? key,
                source: "canvas",
                kind: "url",
                url: src,
                title: title ?? domain ?? null,
                thumbnail_url: null,
                shape_id: shape.id ?? key,
                note: null,
                added_at: addedAt,
                ...(isDuplicate ? { duplicate: true } : {}),
              });
            }
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // --- Map attached_pdfs ---
  for (const pdf of attached_pdfs) {
    attachedEntries.push({
      id: pdf.id,
      source: "attached_pdf",
      kind: "pdf",
      url: pdf.storage_key, // storage_key is the canonical reference; public URL built in display layer
      title: pdf.filename,
      thumbnail_url: null,
      filename: pdf.filename,
      size_bytes: pdf.size_bytes,
      note: null,
      added_at: pdf.uploaded_at,
    });
  }

  // --- Map attached_urls ---
  for (const urlEntry of attached_urls) {
    attachedEntries.push({
      id: urlEntry.id,
      source: "attached_url",
      kind: "url",
      url: urlEntry.url,
      title: urlEntry.title,
      thumbnail_url: urlEntry.thumbnail_url,
      provider: urlEntry.provider,
      note: urlEntry.note,
      added_at: urlEntry.added_at,
    });
  }

  // --- Sort each group by added_at ascending ---
  const sortByAddedAt = (a: AssetIndexEntry, b: AssetIndexEntry) =>
    a.added_at.localeCompare(b.added_at);

  attachedEntries.sort(sortByAddedAt);
  canvasEntries.sort(sortByAddedAt);

  // --- Result: attached first, then canvas ---
  return [...attachedEntries, ...canvasEntries];
}

/**
 * board-actions.ts
 * Phase 3.1 task_05 ??server actions for ProjectBoard brief mode.
 *
 * Three actions:
 *   - updateProjectBoardAction(projectId, document)
 *       Validates auth + lock state; recomputes asset_index server-side
 *       (K-05 trust boundary ??never trust client-supplied asset_index);
 *       inserts a project_board_versions snapshot if >30s since last;
 *       updates project_boards.{document, asset_index, updated_at}.
 *
 *   - toggleLockAction(boardId, locked)
 *       Wraps toggle_project_board_lock RPC (SECURITY DEFINER, yagi_admin only).
 *
 *   - restoreVersionAction(boardId, version)
 *       Admin-only; copies project_board_versions.document back into
 *       project_boards.document and recomputes asset_index.
 *
 * All anti-DoS: 5MB serialized cap on document.
 */

import { z } from "zod";
import { revalidatePath } from "next/cache";
import { createSupabaseServer } from "@/lib/supabase/server";
import { createSupabaseService } from "@/lib/supabase/service";
import { extractAssetIndex } from "@/lib/board/asset-index";
import {
  createBriefAssetPutUrl,
  briefObjectPublicUrl,
} from "@/lib/r2/client";
import { fetchVideoMetadata } from "@/lib/oembed";

const VERSION_DEBOUNCE_MS = 30_000;
const DOCUMENT_MAX_BYTES = 5 * 1024 * 1024;

// K-05 LOOP 1 MEDIUM F6 fix: same validator as wizard's submitProjectAction
// to reject malformed tldraw store snapshots. Empty {} is permitted (a brief
// in initial state). Otherwise document MUST contain a `store` object key.
function validateTldrawStore(doc: Record<string, unknown>): boolean {
  if (!doc || typeof doc !== "object") return false;
  if (Object.keys(doc).length === 0) return true;
  if (!("store" in doc)) return false;
  const store = (doc as { store: unknown }).store;
  if (typeof store !== "object" || store === null) return false;
  return true;
}

// ============================================================
// updateProjectBoardAction
// ============================================================

const UpdateBoardSchema = z.object({
  projectId: z.string().uuid(),
  document: z
    .record(z.string(), z.unknown())
    .refine(validateTldrawStore, {
      message: "document is not a valid tldraw store snapshot",
    }),
});

export type UpdateBoardResult =
  | { ok: true; boardId: string }
  | {
      ok: false;
      error: "unauthenticated" | "validation" | "locked" | "not_found" | "db";
      message?: string;
    };

export async function updateProjectBoardAction(
  input: unknown
): Promise<UpdateBoardResult> {
  const parsed = UpdateBoardSchema.safeParse(input);
  if (!parsed.success) return { ok: false, error: "validation" };

  // Anti-DoS
  let serialized: string;
  try {
    serialized = JSON.stringify(parsed.data.document);
  } catch {
    return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
  }
  if (serialized.length > DOCUMENT_MAX_BYTES) {
    return { ok: false, error: "validation", message: "document_too_large" };
  }

  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };

  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
  const sb = supabase as any;

  // Fetch the board (RLS gates SELECT ??non-owner non-admin gets nothing)
  const { data: board, error: bErr } = await sb
    .from("project_boards")
    .select("id, is_locked")
    .eq("project_id", parsed.data.projectId)
    .maybeSingle();
  if (bErr || !board) return { ok: false, error: "not_found" };
  if (board.is_locked) return { ok: false, error: "locked" };

  // K-05 trust boundary: server-recompute asset_index. Never trust client.
  // Phase 3.1 hotfix-3: also merge attached_pdfs + attached_urls (read from DB).
  // For canvas-only update, fetch current attachment state from DB to merge.
  const { data: currentBoard } = await sb
    .from("project_boards")
    .select("attached_pdfs, attached_urls")
    .eq("id", board.id)
    .maybeSingle();
  const assetIndex = extractAssetIndex(
    parsed.data.document,
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 columns not in generated types
    ((currentBoard as any)?.attached_pdfs ?? []) as any,
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 columns not in generated types
    ((currentBoard as any)?.attached_urls ?? []) as any,
  );

  // K-05 LOOP 1 HIGH-B F3 fix: atomic update guarded by is_locked=false to
  // close the lock race window. If admin locks between our SELECT and UPDATE,
  // the WHERE clause filters it out and `updated` returns empty rows; we then
  // return error:locked WITHOUT having inserted a version snapshot.
  const { data: updated, error: uErr } = await sb
    .from("project_boards")
    .update({
      document: parsed.data.document,
      asset_index: assetIndex,
      updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    })
    .eq("id", board.id)
    .eq("is_locked", false)
    .select("id");
  if (uErr) {
    console.error("[updateProjectBoardAction] update error:", uErr);
    return { ok: false, error: "db", message: uErr.message };
  }
  if (!Array.isArray(updated) || updated.length === 0) {
    // Lock was acquired between SELECT and UPDATE ??no rows updated, no snapshot.
    return { ok: false, error: "locked" };
  }

  // Versioning: snapshot AFTER successful update (K-05 LOOP 1 HIGH-B F3 fix ??  // never insert a version row for a write that did not land).
  const { data: lastVersion } = await sb
    .from("project_board_versions")
    .select("created_at, version")
    .eq("board_id", board.id)
    .order("version", { ascending: false })
    .limit(1)
    .maybeSingle();

  const shouldSnapshot =
    !lastVersion ||
    Date.now() - new Date(lastVersion.created_at as string).getTime() >
      VERSION_DEBOUNCE_MS;

  if (shouldSnapshot) {
    const nextVersion = ((lastVersion?.version as number | undefined) ?? 0) + 1;
    // INSERT bypasses RLS via service role (project_board_versions_insert_trigger
    // has WITH CHECK false, so user-scoped client cannot INSERT directly).
    const svc = createSupabaseService();
    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
    await (svc as any).from("project_board_versions").insert({
      board_id: board.id,
      version: nextVersion,
      document: parsed.data.document,
      created_by: user.id,
      label: null,
    });
  }

  revalidatePath(`/[locale]/app/projects/${parsed.data.projectId}`, "page");
  return { ok: true, boardId: board.id };
}

// ============================================================
// toggleLockAction
// ============================================================

const ToggleLockSchema = z.object({
  boardId: z.string().uuid(),
  locked: z.boolean(),
});

export type ToggleLockResult =
  | { ok: true }
  | {
      ok: false;
      error: "unauthenticated" | "validation" | "db" | "forbidden";
      message?: string;
    };

export async function toggleLockAction(
  input: unknown
): Promise<ToggleLockResult> {
  const parsed = ToggleLockSchema.safeParse(input);
  if (!parsed.success) return { ok: false, error: "validation" };

  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };

  // RPC enforces yagi_admin internally (RAISE EXCEPTION if not admin).
  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1: RPC not in generated types
  const { error } = await (supabase as any).rpc("toggle_project_board_lock", {
    p_board_id: parsed.data.boardId,
    p_locked: parsed.data.locked,
  });
  if (error) {
    console.error("[toggleLockAction] rpc error:", error);
    return { ok: false, error: "db", message: error.message };
  }
  return { ok: true };
}

// ============================================================
// toggleBoardLockAction (Phase 3.1 hotfix-3 task_04)
// Defense-in-depth: action verifies yagi_admin role + RPC verifies.
// ============================================================

export type ToggleBoardLockResult =
  | { ok: true; isLocked: boolean }
  | {
      ok: false;
      error: "unauthenticated" | "forbidden" | "validation" | "db";
      message?: string;
    };

export async function toggleBoardLockAction(
  boardId: string,
  locked: boolean
): Promise<ToggleBoardLockResult> {
  if (!boardId || typeof boardId !== "string") {
    return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
  }
  if (typeof locked !== "boolean") {
    return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
  }

  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
  const {
    data: { user },
  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };

  // Action-layer role check (defense-in-depth over RPC-only check)
  const { data: roles } = await supabase
    .from("user_roles")
    .select("role")
    .eq("user_id", user.id);
  const isYagiAdmin = (roles ?? []).some(
    (r) => (r as { role: string }).role === "yagi_admin"
  );
  if (!isYagiAdmin) return { ok: false, error: "forbidden" };

  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1: RPC not in generated types

-- Phase 3.1 hotfix-3: attached_pdfs + attached_urls columns + 4 attachment RPCs + extend seed RPC
-- Execution: additive only -- ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS with safe defaults
-- Recorded version: to be confirmed via L-021 after MCP apply_migration

-- ============================================================
-- Schema changes: add attachment columns to project_boards
-- ============================================================
ALTER TABLE project_boards
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS attached_pdfs jsonb NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]'::jsonb,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS attached_urls jsonb NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]'::jsonb;

-- ============================================================
-- RPC: add_project_board_pdf
-- Appends a PDF attachment entry to project_boards.attached_pdfs.
-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state, count cap (30),
-- size cap (20MB), filename length (200), storage_key prefix.
-- SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked to public, pg_temp.
-- Does NOT update asset_index (that is server action layer responsibility).
-- ============================================================
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION add_project_board_pdf(
  p_board_id    uuid,
  p_storage_key text,
  p_filename    text,
  p_size_bytes  bigint
) RETURNS uuid
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public, pg_temp
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
  v_project_id uuid;
  v_is_locked  boolean;
  v_is_admin   boolean;
  v_new_id     uuid := gen_random_uuid();
  v_pdf_count  int;
BEGIN
  -- Fetch board meta
  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
  FROM project_boards pb
  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: board not found';
  END IF;

  -- Role check: owner OR yagi_admin
  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
  ) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: unauthorized';
  END IF;

  -- Lock check: block non-admin mutations on locked board
  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: board is locked';
  END IF;

  -- Count cap: max 30 PDFs
  SELECT jsonb_array_length(attached_pdfs) INTO v_pdf_count
  FROM project_boards WHERE id = p_board_id;
  IF v_pdf_count >= 30 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: PDF count limit reached (max 30)';
  END IF;

  -- Size cap: max 20MB
  IF p_size_bytes > 20 * 1024 * 1024 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: file too large (max 20MB)';
  END IF;

  -- Filename length
  IF p_filename IS NULL OR length(p_filename) = 0 OR length(p_filename) > 200 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: filename must be 1-200 chars';
  END IF;

  -- Storage key prefix validation: no path traversal, no absolute path, must start with known prefix
  IF p_storage_key IS NULL
    OR p_storage_key LIKE '%..%'
    OR left(p_storage_key, 1) = '/'
    OR (p_storage_key NOT LIKE 'project-wizard/%' AND p_storage_key NOT LIKE 'project-board/%') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: invalid storage_key (must start with project-wizard/ or project-board/)';
  END IF;

  -- Append entry using jsonb_build_object (no string concatenation)
  UPDATE project_boards
  SET
    attached_pdfs = attached_pdfs || jsonb_build_array(
      jsonb_build_object(
        'id',          v_new_id::text,
        'storage_key', p_storage_key,
        'filename',    p_filename,
        'size_bytes',  p_size_bytes,
        'uploaded_at', now()::text,
        'uploaded_by', v_caller_id::text
      )
    ),
    updated_at = now()
  WHERE id = p_board_id;

  RETURN v_new_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- RPC: add_project_board_url
-- Appends a URL attachment entry to project_boards.attached_urls.
-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state, count cap (50),
-- URL scheme (http/https only), URL length (2000), note length (500),
-- provider enum (youtube/vimeo/generic).
-- SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked to public, pg_temp.
-- ============================================================
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION add_project_board_url(
  p_board_id      uuid,
  p_url           text,
  p_title         text,
  p_thumbnail_url text,
  p_provider      text,
  p_note          text
) RETURNS uuid
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public, pg_temp
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
  v_project_id uuid;
  v_is_locked  boolean;
  v_is_admin   boolean;
  v_new_id     uuid := gen_random_uuid();
  v_url_count  int;
BEGIN
  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
  FROM project_boards pb
  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: board not found';
  END IF;

  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
  ) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: unauthorized';
  END IF;

  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: board is locked';
  END IF;

  SELECT jsonb_array_length(attached_urls) INTO v_url_count
  FROM project_boards WHERE id = p_board_id;
  IF v_url_count >= 50 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: URL count limit reached (max 50)';
  END IF;

  -- URL validation: http/https only, max 2000 chars
  -- Explicitly rejects javascript:, data:, file:, chrome:, etc.
  IF p_url IS NULL
    OR length(p_url) > 2000
    OR (p_url NOT LIKE 'http://%' AND p_url NOT LIKE 'https://%') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: invalid URL (must be http:// or https://, max 2000 chars)';
  END IF;

  -- Note length
  IF p_note IS NOT NULL AND length(p_note) > 500 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: note too long (max 500 chars)';
  END IF;

  -- Provider enum validation
  IF p_provider IS NULL OR p_provider NOT IN ('youtube', 'vimeo', 'generic') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: provider must be youtube, vimeo, or generic';
  END IF;

  UPDATE project_boards
  SET
    attached_urls = attached_urls || jsonb_build_array(
      jsonb_build_object(
        'id',            v_new_id::text,
        'url',           p_url,
        'title',         p_title,
        'thumbnail_url', p_thumbnail_url,
        'provider',      p_provider,
        'note',          p_note,
        'added_at',      now()::text,
        'added_by',      v_caller_id::text
      )
    ),
    updated_at = now()
  WHERE id = p_board_id;

  RETURN v_new_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- RPC: remove_project_board_attachment
-- Removes an attachment by id from attached_pdfs or attached_urls.
-- kind must be 'pdf' or 'url'.
-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state.
-- Normalizes null back to empty array if all items removed.
-- ============================================================
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION remove_project_board_attachment(
  p_board_id      uuid,
  p_kind          text,
  p_attachment_id uuid
) RETURNS boolean
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public, pg_temp
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
  v_project_id uuid;
  v_is_locked  boolean;
  v_is_admin   boolean;
BEGIN
  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
  FROM project_boards pb
  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: board not found';
  END IF;

  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
  ) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: unauthorized';
  END IF;

  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: board is locked';
  END IF;

  IF p_kind NOT IN ('pdf', 'url') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: kind must be pdf or url';
  END IF;

  IF p_kind = 'pdf' THEN
    UPDATE project_boards
    SET
      attached_pdfs = COALESCE(
        (
          SELECT jsonb_agg(elem)
          FROM jsonb_array_elements(attached_pdfs) elem
          WHERE (elem->>'id') <> p_attachment_id::text
        ),
        '[]'::jsonb
      ),
      updated_at = now()
    WHERE id = p_board_id;

99:// LockButton component
100:// ============================================================
102:export function LockButton({ boardId: _boardId, isLocked, onToggle }: Props) {
103:  const t = useTranslations("board.lock");
104:  const [optimisticLocked, setOptimisticLocked] = useState(isLocked);
105:  const [showConfirm, setShowConfirm] = useState(false);
106:  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
108:  // Sync if server re-renders with new prop (e.g., after page revalidation)
109:  if (isLocked !== optimisticLocked && !loading) {
110:    setOptimisticLocked(isLocked);
111:  }
113:  const handleClick = () => {
114:    if (optimisticLocked) {
115:      // Unlock: no confirmation needed
116:      void handleToggle(false);
117:    } else {
118:      // Lock: show confirmation first
119:      setShowConfirm(true);
120:    }
121:  };
123:  const handleToggle = async (newState: boolean) => {
124:    setLoading(true);
125:    setOptimisticLocked(newState); // optimistic
126:    const result = await onToggle(newState);
127:    if (!result.ok) {
128:      // Roll back optimistic
129:      setOptimisticLocked(!newState);
130:      console.error("[LockButton] toggle failed");
131:    }
132:    setLoading(false);
133:  };
135:  return (
136:    <>
137:      <button
138:        type="button"
139:        onClick={handleClick}
140:        disabled={loading}
141:        aria-label={
142:          optimisticLocked
143:            ? t("unlock_button")
144:            : t("lock_button")
145:        }
146:        className={[
147:          "font-suit text-xs rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 transition-colors disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center gap-1.5",
148:          optimisticLocked
149:            ? // Filled (locked state) — achromatic, no color
150:              "border border-border/60 bg-foreground text-background hover:opacity-90"
151:            : // Outline (unlocked state)
152:              "border border-border/40 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-muted",
153:        ]
154:          .filter(Boolean)
155:          .join(" ")}
156:        style={{ boxShadow: "0 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.04)" }}
157:      >
158:        {optimisticLocked ? t("unlock_button") : t("lock_button")}
159:      </button>
161:      {showConfirm && (
162:        <ConfirmDialog
163:          onConfirm={() => {
164:            setShowConfirm(false);
165:            void handleToggle(true);
166:          }}
167:          onCancel={() => setShowConfirm(false)}
168:        />
169:      )}
170:    </>
171:  );
172:}

44:// ============================================================
45:// URL validation helpers (client-side, L-042)
46:// ============================================================
48:const BLOCKED_SCHEMES = ["javascript:", "data:", "file:", "chrome:", "blob:", "vbscript:"];
50:function isValidUrl(raw: string): { valid: boolean; reason?: string } {
51:  let parsed: URL;
52:  try {
53:    parsed = new URL(raw);
54:  } catch {
55:    return { valid: false, reason: "parse_error" };
56:  }
58:  // Only http/https allowed
59:  if (parsed.protocol !== "http:" && parsed.protocol !== "https:") {
60:    return { valid: false, reason: "scheme" };
61:  }
63:  // Belt-and-suspenders: explicitly reject dangerous schemes even if above passes
64:  const lower = raw.toLowerCase().trim();
65:  for (const blocked of BLOCKED_SCHEMES) {
66:    if (lower.startsWith(blocked)) {
67:      return { valid: false, reason: "scheme" };
68:    }
69:  }
71:  return { valid: true };
72:}
74:function detectProvider(url: string): UrlAttachment["provider"] {
75:  try {
76:    const parsed = new URL(url);
77:    const host = parsed.hostname.replace(/^www\./, "");
78:    if (host === "youtube.com" || host === "youtu.be") return "youtube";
79:    if (host === "vimeo.com") return "vimeo";
80:  } catch {
81:    // ignore
82:  }
83:  return "generic";
84:}

94:  onPdfRemove,
95:  onUrlAdd,
96:  onUrlNoteUpdate,
97:  onUrlRemove,
98:  isLocked,
99:  isReadOnly,
100:}: Props) {
101:  const t = useTranslations("attachments");
102:  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
104:  // URL form state
105:  const [urlInput, setUrlInput] = useState("");
106:  const [noteInput, setNoteInput] = useState("");
107:  const [urlError, setUrlError] = useState("");
108:  const [urlSubmitting, setUrlSubmitting] = useState(false);
110:  // PDF drag state
111:  const [pdfDragActive, setPdfDragActive] = useState(false);
112:  const [pdfError, setPdfError] = useState("");
113:  const [pdfUploading, setPdfUploading] = useState(false);
115:  const mutationsDisabled = isLocked || isReadOnly;
117:  // ============================================================
118:  // PDF handlers
119:  // ============================================================
121:  const PDF_MAX_BYTES = 20 * 1024 * 1024; // 20MB (L-042: per task_01 RPC)
122:  const PDF_MAX_COUNT = 30;
124:  async function handlePdfFile(file: File) {
125:    setPdfError("");
127:    if (file.type !== "application/pdf") {
128:      setPdfError("PDF 파일만 업로드 가능합니다.");
129:      return;
130:    }
132:    if (file.size > PDF_MAX_BYTES) {
133:      setPdfError(t("pdf.size_too_large"));
134:      return;
135:    }
137:    if (pdfs.length >= PDF_MAX_COUNT) {
138:      setPdfError(t("pdf.count_exceeded"));
139:      return;
140:    }
142:    setPdfUploading(true);
143:    try {
144:      await onPdfAdd(file);
145:    } catch (err) {
146:      console.error("[AttachmentsSection] PDF add failed:", err);
147:      setPdfError("업로드 중 오류가 발생했습니다. 다시 시도해주세요.");
148:    } finally {
149:      setPdfUploading(false);
150:    }
151:  }
153:  function handleFilePickerChange(e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) {
154:    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
155:    if (file) handlePdfFile(file);
156:    // Reset input so the same file can be re-selected
157:    e.target.value = "";
158:  }
160:  function handlePdfDragOver(e: React.DragEvent<HTMLDivElement>) {
161:    e.preventDefault();
162:    if (!mutationsDisabled) setPdfDragActive(true);
163:  }
165:  function handlePdfDragLeave() {
166:    setPdfDragActive(false);
167:  }
169:  async function handlePdfDrop(e: React.DragEvent<HTMLDivElement>) {
170:    e.preventDefault();
171:    setPdfDragActive(false);
172:    if (mutationsDisabled) return;
174:    const file = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files).find(
175:      (f) => f.type === "application/pdf"
176:    );
177:    if (file) await handlePdfFile(file);
178:  }
180:  // ============================================================
181:  // URL handlers
182:  // ============================================================
184:  const URL_MAX_COUNT = 50;
186:  async function handleUrlSubmit(e: React.FormEvent) {
187:    e.preventDefault();
188:    setUrlError("");
190:    const trimmed = urlInput.trim();
191:    const { valid } = isValidUrl(trimmed);
193:    if (!valid) {
194:      setUrlError(t("url.invalid"));
195:      return;
196:    }
198:    if (urls.length >= URL_MAX_COUNT) {
199:      setUrlError(t("url.count_exceeded"));
200:      return;
201:    }
203:    setUrlSubmitting(true);
204:    try {
205:      await onUrlAdd(trimmed, noteInput.trim() || null);
206:      setUrlInput("");
207:      setNoteInput("");
208:    } catch (err) {
209:      console.error("[AttachmentsSection] URL add failed:", err);
210:      setUrlError("링크 추가 중 오류가 발생했습니다.");
211:    } finally {
212:      setUrlSubmitting(false);
213:    }
214:  }
216:  function handleUrlNoteUpdate(id: string, note: string) {
217:    onUrlNoteUpdate(id, note).catch((err) => {
218:      console.error("[AttachmentsSection] URL note update failed:", err);
219:    });
220:  }
222:  // ============================================================
223:  // Render
224:  // ============================================================
226:  return (
227:    <div className="space-y-0">
228:      {/* ─────────────────── PDF SECTION ─────────────────── */}
229:      <section
230:        onDragOver={handlePdfDragOver}
231:        onDragLeave={handlePdfDragLeave}
232:        onDrop={handlePdfDrop}
233:        className={[
234:          "py-6 rounded-md transition-colors",
235:          pdfDragActive ? "bg-muted/40" : "",
236:        ]
237:          .filter(Boolean)
238:          .join(" ")}
239:        aria-label="PDF attachments"
240:      >
241:        {/* Eyebrow — L-010: font-suit text-xs uppercase tracking-wider */}
242:        <p className="font-suit text-[11px] font-semibold tracking-[0.12em] uppercase text-muted-foreground/70 mb-1">
243:          {t("pdf.eyebrow")}
244:        </p>
245:        <p className="font-suit text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">
246:          {t("pdf.sub")}
247:        </p>
249:        {/* Add button */}
250:        {!mutationsDisabled && (
251:          <div className="mb-4">
252:            <button
253:              type="button"
254:              onClick={() => fileInputRef.current?.click()}
255:              disabled={pdfUploading}
256:              className="font-suit text-sm rounded-md px-4 py-2 border border-border/40 text-foreground hover:bg-muted transition-colors disabled:opacity-50"
257:              style={{
258:                boxShadow:
259:                  "0 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.04)",
260:              }}
261:            >
262:              {pdfUploading ? "업로드 중..." : t("pdf.add")}
263:            </button>
264:            {/* Hidden file input */}
265:            <input
266:              ref={fileInputRef}
267:              type="file"
268:              accept=".pdf,application/pdf"
269:              className="hidden"
270:              onChange={handleFilePickerChange}
271:              aria-label="PDF file picker"
272:            />
273:          </div>
274:        )}
276:        {/* Error message */}
277:        {pdfError && (
278:          <p className="font-suit text-xs text-foreground mb-3 px-1">
279:            {pdfError}
280:          </p>
281:        )}
283:        {/* PDF card list */}
284:        {pdfs.length > 0 ? (
285:          <div className="space-y-2">
286:            {pdfs.map((pdf) => (
287:              <PdfCard
288:                key={pdf.id}
289:                pdf={pdf}
290:                onRemove={onPdfRemove}
291:                disabled={mutationsDisabled}
292:              />
293:            ))}
294:          </div>
295:        ) : (
296:          <p className="font-suit text-sm text-muted-foreground/60">
297:            {t("pdf.empty")}
298:          </p>
299:        )}
300:      </section>
302:      {/* Hairline divider between sections — L-012: no section backgrounds */}
303:      <hr className="border-t border-border/30" />
305:      {/* ─────────────────── URL SECTION ─────────────────── */}
306:      <section className="py-6" aria-label="URL attachments">
307:        {/* Eyebrow — L-010 */}
308:        <p className="font-suit text-[11px] font-semibold tracking-[0.12em] uppercase text-muted-foreground/70 mb-1">
309:          {t("url.eyebrow")}
310:        </p>
311:        <p className="font-suit text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">
312:          {t("url.sub")}
313:        </p>
315:        {/* Inline URL form */}
316:        {!mutationsDisabled && (
317:          <form onSubmit={handleUrlSubmit} className="mb-4 space-y-2">
318:            <div className="flex gap-2">
319:              <input
320:                type="url"
321:                value={urlInput}
322:                onChange={(e) => {
323:                  setUrlInput(e.target.value);
324:                  if (urlError) setUrlError("");
325:                }}
326:                placeholder={t("url.placeholder")}
327:                className="flex-1 font-suit text-sm rounded-md px-3 py-2 border border-border/40 bg-background placeholder:text-muted-foreground/60 focus:outline-none focus:rin

328:                aria-label="URL input"

335:              >

341:            {urlInput.trim() && (
342:              <input
343:                type="text"
344:                value={noteInput}
345:                onChange={(e) => setNoteInput(e.target.value)}
346:                placeholder={t("url.note_placeholder")}
347:                maxLength={500}
348:                className="w-full font-suit text-sm rounded-md px-3 py-2 border border-border/40 bg-background placeholder:text-muted-foreground/60 focus:outline-none focus:rin

12:-- ============================================================
13:-- RPC: add_project_board_pdf
14:-- Appends a PDF attachment entry to project_boards.attached_pdfs.
15:-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state, count cap (30),
16:-- size cap (20MB), filename length (200), storage_key prefix.
17:-- SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked to public, pg_temp.
18:-- Does NOT update asset_index (that is server action layer responsibility).
19:-- ============================================================
20:CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION add_project_board_pdf(
21:  p_board_id    uuid,
22:  p_storage_key text,
23:  p_filename    text,
24:  p_size_bytes  bigint
25:) RETURNS uuid
26:LANGUAGE plpgsql
27:SECURITY DEFINER
28:SET search_path = public, pg_temp
29:AS $$
30:DECLARE
31:  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
32:  v_project_id uuid;
33:  v_is_locked  boolean;
34:  v_is_admin   boolean;
35:  v_new_id     uuid := gen_random_uuid();
36:  v_pdf_count  int;
37:BEGIN
38:  -- Fetch board meta
39:  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
40:  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
41:  FROM project_boards pb
42:  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;
44:  IF NOT FOUND THEN
45:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: board not found';
46:  END IF;
48:  -- Role check: owner OR yagi_admin
49:  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
50:  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
51:    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
52:    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
53:  ) THEN
54:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: unauthorized';
55:  END IF;
57:  -- Lock check: block non-admin mutations on locked board
58:  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
59:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: board is locked';
60:  END IF;
62:  -- Count cap: max 30 PDFs
63:  SELECT jsonb_array_length(attached_pdfs) INTO v_pdf_count
64:  FROM project_boards WHERE id = p_board_id;
65:  IF v_pdf_count >= 30 THEN
66:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: PDF count limit reached (max 30)';
67:  END IF;
69:  -- Size cap: max 20MB
70:  IF p_size_bytes > 20 * 1024 * 1024 THEN
71:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: file too large (max 20MB)';
72:  END IF;
74:  -- Filename length
75:  IF p_filename IS NULL OR length(p_filename) = 0 OR length(p_filename) > 200 THEN
76:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: filename must be 1-200 chars';
77:  END IF;
79:  -- Storage key prefix validation: no path traversal, no absolute path, must start with known prefix
80:  IF p_storage_key IS NULL
81:    OR p_storage_key LIKE '%..%'
82:    OR left(p_storage_key, 1) = '/'
83:    OR (p_storage_key NOT LIKE 'project-wizard/%' AND p_storage_key NOT LIKE 'project-board/%') THEN
84:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_pdf: invalid storage_key (must start with project-wizard/ or project-board/)';
85:  END IF;
87:  -- Append entry using jsonb_build_object (no string concatenation)
88:  UPDATE project_boards
89:  SET
90:    attached_pdfs = attached_pdfs || jsonb_build_array(
91:      jsonb_build_object(
92:        'id',          v_new_id::text,
93:        'storage_key', p_storage_key,
94:        'filename',    p_filename,
95:        'size_bytes',  p_size_bytes,
96:        'uploaded_at', now()::text,
97:        'uploaded_by', v_caller_id::text
98:      )
99:    ),
100:    updated_at = now()
101:  WHERE id = p_board_id;
103:  RETURN v_new_id;
104:END;
105:$$;
107:-- ============================================================
108:-- RPC: add_project_board_url
109:-- Appends a URL attachment entry to project_boards.attached_urls.
110:-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state, count cap (50),
111:-- URL scheme (http/https only), URL length (2000), note length (500),
112:-- provider enum (youtube/vimeo/generic).
113:-- SECURITY DEFINER, search_path locked to public, pg_temp.
114:-- ============================================================
115:CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION add_project_board_url(
116:  p_board_id      uuid,
117:  p_url           text,
118:  p_title         text,
119:  p_thumbnail_url text,
120:  p_provider      text,
121:  p_note          text
122:) RETURNS uuid
123:LANGUAGE plpgsql
124:SECURITY DEFINER
125:SET search_path = public, pg_temp
126:AS $$
127:DECLARE
128:  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
129:  v_project_id uuid;
130:  v_is_locked  boolean;
131:  v_is_admin   boolean;
132:  v_new_id     uuid := gen_random_uuid();
133:  v_url_count  int;
134:BEGIN
135:  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
136:  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
137:  FROM project_boards pb
138:  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;
140:  IF NOT FOUND THEN
141:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: board not found';
142:  END IF;
144:  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
145:  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
146:    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
147:    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
148:  ) THEN
149:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: unauthorized';
150:  END IF;
152:  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
153:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: board is locked';
154:  END IF;
156:  SELECT jsonb_array_length(attached_urls) INTO v_url_count
157:  FROM project_boards WHERE id = p_board_id;
158:  IF v_url_count >= 50 THEN
159:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: URL count limit reached (max 50)';
160:  END IF;
162:  -- URL validation: http/https only, max 2000 chars
163:  -- Explicitly rejects javascript:, data:, file:, chrome:, etc.
164:  IF p_url IS NULL
165:    OR length(p_url) > 2000
166:    OR (p_url NOT LIKE 'http://%' AND p_url NOT LIKE 'https://%') THEN
167:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: invalid URL (must be http:// or https://, max 2000 chars)';
168:  END IF;
170:  -- Note length
171:  IF p_note IS NOT NULL AND length(p_note) > 500 THEN
172:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: note too long (max 500 chars)';
173:  END IF;
175:  -- Provider enum validation
176:  IF p_provider IS NULL OR p_provider NOT IN ('youtube', 'vimeo', 'generic') THEN
177:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'add_project_board_url: provider must be youtube, vimeo, or generic';
178:  END IF;
180:  UPDATE project_boards
181:  SET
182:    attached_urls = attached_urls || jsonb_build_array(
183:      jsonb_build_object(
184:        'id',            v_new_id::text,
185:        'url',           p_url,
186:        'title',         p_title,
187:        'thumbnail_url', p_thumbnail_url,
188:        'provider',      p_provider,
189:        'note',          p_note,
190:        'added_at',      now()::text,
191:        'added_by',      v_caller_id::text
192:      )
193:    ),
194:    updated_at = now()
195:  WHERE id = p_board_id;
197:  RETURN v_new_id;
198:END;
199:$$;
201:-- ============================================================
202:-- RPC: remove_project_board_attachment
203:-- Removes an attachment by id from attached_pdfs or attached_urls.
204:-- kind must be 'pdf' or 'url'.
205:-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state.
206:-- Normalizes null back to empty array if all items removed.
207:-- ============================================================
208:CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION remove_project_board_attachment(
209:  p_board_id      uuid,
210:  p_kind          text,
211:  p_attachment_id uuid
212:) RETURNS boolean
213:LANGUAGE plpgsql
214:SECURITY DEFINER
215:SET search_path = public, pg_temp
216:AS $$
217:DECLARE
218:  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
219:  v_project_id uuid;
220:  v_is_locked  boolean;
221:  v_is_admin   boolean;
222:BEGIN
223:  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
224:  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
225:  FROM project_boards pb
226:  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;
228:  IF NOT FOUND THEN
229:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: board not found';
230:  END IF;
232:  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
233:  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
234:    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
235:    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
236:  ) THEN
237:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: unauthorized';
238:  END IF;
240:  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
241:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: board is locked';
242:  END IF;
244:  IF p_kind NOT IN ('pdf', 'url') THEN
245:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'remove_project_board_attachment: kind must be pdf or url';
246:  END IF;
248:  IF p_kind = 'pdf' THEN
249:    UPDATE project_boards
250:    SET
251:      attached_pdfs = COALESCE(
252:        (
253:          SELECT jsonb_agg(elem)
254:          FROM jsonb_array_elements(attached_pdfs) elem
255:          WHERE (elem->>'id') <> p_attachment_id::text
256:        ),
257:        '[]'::jsonb
258:      ),
259:      updated_at = now()
260:    WHERE id = p_board_id;
261:  ELSE
262:    UPDATE project_boards
263:    SET
264:      attached_urls = COALESCE(
265:        (
266:          SELECT jsonb_agg(elem)
267:          FROM jsonb_array_elements(attached_urls) elem
268:          WHERE (elem->>'id') <> p_attachment_id::text
269:        ),
270:        '[]'::jsonb
271:      ),
272:      updated_at = now()
273:    WHERE id = p_board_id;
274:  END IF;
276:  RETURN true;
277:END;
278:$$;
280:-- ============================================================
281:-- RPC: update_project_board_url_note
282:-- Updates the note field of a URL attachment (URL itself is immutable).
283:-- Validates: caller ownership OR yagi_admin, lock state, note length (500).
284:-- ============================================================
285:CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_project_board_url_note(
286:  p_board_id      uuid,
287:  p_attachment_id uuid,
288:  p_note          text
289:) RETURNS boolean
290:LANGUAGE plpgsql
291:SECURITY DEFINER
292:SET search_path = public, pg_temp
293:AS $$
294:DECLARE
295:  v_caller_id  uuid := auth.uid();
296:  v_project_id uuid;
297:  v_is_locked  boolean;
298:  v_is_admin   boolean;
299:BEGIN
300:  SELECT pb.project_id, pb.is_locked
301:  INTO v_project_id, v_is_locked
302:  FROM project_boards pb
303:  WHERE pb.id = p_board_id;
305:  IF NOT FOUND THEN
306:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'update_project_board_url_note: board not found';
307:  END IF;
309:  v_is_admin := is_yagi_admin(v_caller_id);
310:  IF NOT v_is_admin AND NOT EXISTS (
311:    SELECT 1 FROM projects p
312:    WHERE p.id = v_project_id AND p.owner_id = v_caller_id
313:  ) THEN
314:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'update_project_board_url_note: unauthorized';
315:  END IF;
317:  IF v_is_locked AND NOT v_is_admin THEN
318:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'update_project_board_url_note: board is locked';
319:  END IF;
321:  IF p_note IS NOT NULL AND length(p_note) > 500 THEN
322:    RAISE EXCEPTION 'update_project_board_url_note: note too long (max 500 chars)';
323:  END IF;
325:  UPDATE project_boards
326:  SET
327:    attached_urls = (
328:      SELECT jsonb_agg(
329:        CASE
330:          WHEN (elem->>'id') = p_attachment_id::text
331:          THEN jsonb_set(elem, '{note}', COALESCE(to_jsonb(p_note), 'null'::jsonb))
332:          ELSE elem
333:        END
334:      )
335:      FROM jsonb_array_elements(attached_urls) elem
336:    ),
337:    updated_at = now()
338:  WHERE id = p_board_id;
340:  RETURN true;
341:END;
342:$$;
344:-- ============================================================
345:-- RPC: seed_project_board_from_wizard (EXTEND signature)

349:-- ============================================================
350:CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION seed_project_board_from_wizard(

35:const VERSION_DEBOUNCE_MS = 30_000;

38:// K-05 LOOP 1 MEDIUM F6 fix: same validator as wizard's submitProjectAction
39:// to reject malformed tldraw store snapshots. Empty {} is permitted (a brief
40:// in initial state). Otherwise document MUST contain a `store` object key.
41:function validateTldrawStore(doc: Record<string, unknown>): boolean {
42:  if (!doc || typeof doc !== "object") return false;
43:  if (Object.keys(doc).length === 0) return true;
44:  if (!("store" in doc)) return false;
45:  const store = (doc as { store: unknown }).store;
46:  if (typeof store !== "object" || store === null) return false;
47:  return true;
48:}

54:const UpdateBoardSchema = z.object({
55:  projectId: z.string().uuid(),
56:  document: z
57:    .record(z.string(), z.unknown())
58:    .refine(validateTldrawStore, {
59:      message: "document is not a valid tldraw store snapshot",
60:    }),
61:});
63:export type UpdateBoardResult =
64:  | { ok: true; boardId: string }
65:  | {
66:      ok: false;
67:      error: "unauthenticated" | "validation" | "locked" | "not_found" | "db";
68:      message?: string;
69:    };
71:export async function updateProjectBoardAction(
72:  input: unknown
73:): Promise<UpdateBoardResult> {
74:  const parsed = UpdateBoardSchema.safeParse(input);
75:  if (!parsed.success) return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
77:  // Anti-DoS
78:  let serialized: string;
79:  try {
80:    serialized = JSON.stringify(parsed.data.document);
81:  } catch {
82:    return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
83:  }
84:  if (serialized.length > DOCUMENT_MAX_BYTES) {
85:    return { ok: false, error: "validation", message: "document_too_large" };
86:  }
88:  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
89:  const {
90:    data: { user },
91:  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
92:  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };
94:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
95:  const sb = supabase as any;
97:  // Fetch the board (RLS gates SELECT — non-owner non-admin gets nothing)
98:  const { data: board, error: bErr } = await sb
99:    .from("project_boards")
100:    .select("id, is_locked")
101:    .eq("project_id", parsed.data.projectId)
102:    .maybeSingle();
103:  if (bErr || !board) return { ok: false, error: "not_found" };
104:  if (board.is_locked) return { ok: false, error: "locked" };
106:  // K-05 trust boundary: server-recompute asset_index. Never trust client.
107:  // Phase 3.1 hotfix-3: also merge attached_pdfs + attached_urls (read from DB).
108:  // For canvas-only update, fetch current attachment state from DB to merge.
109:  const { data: currentBoard } = await sb
110:    .from("project_boards")
111:    .select("attached_pdfs, attached_urls")
112:    .eq("id", board.id)
113:    .maybeSingle();
114:  const assetIndex = extractAssetIndex(
115:    parsed.data.document,
116:    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 columns not in generated types
117:    ((currentBoard as any)?.attached_pdfs ?? []) as any,
118:    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 columns not in generated types
119:    ((currentBoard as any)?.attached_urls ?? []) as any,
120:  );
122:  // K-05 LOOP 1 HIGH-B F3 fix: atomic update guarded by is_locked=false to
123:  // close the lock race window. If admin locks between our SELECT and UPDATE,
124:  // the WHERE clause filters it out and `updated` returns empty rows; we then
125:  // return error:locked WITHOUT having inserted a version snapshot.
126:  const { data: updated, error: uErr } = await sb
127:    .from("project_boards")
128:    .update({
129:      document: parsed.data.document,
130:      asset_index: assetIndex,
131:      updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
132:    })
133:    .eq("id", board.id)
134:    .eq("is_locked", false)
135:    .select("id");
136:  if (uErr) {
137:    console.error("[updateProjectBoardAction] update error:", uErr);
138:    return { ok: false, error: "db", message: uErr.message };
139:  }
140:  if (!Array.isArray(updated) || updated.length === 0) {
141:    // Lock was acquired between SELECT and UPDATE → no rows updated, no snapshot.
142:    return { ok: false, error: "locked" };
143:  }
145:  // Versioning: snapshot AFTER successful update (K-05 LOOP 1 HIGH-B F3 fix —
146:  // never insert a version row for a write that did not land).
147:  const { data: lastVersion } = await sb
148:    .from("project_board_versions")
149:    .select("created_at, version")
150:    .eq("board_id", board.id)
151:    .order("version", { ascending: false })
152:    .limit(1)
153:    .maybeSingle();
155:  const shouldSnapshot =
156:    !lastVersion ||
157:    Date.now() - new Date(lastVersion.created_at as string).getTime() >
158:      VERSION_DEBOUNCE_MS;
160:  if (shouldSnapshot) {
161:    const nextVersion = ((lastVersion?.version as number | undefined) ?? 0) + 1;
162:    // INSERT bypasses RLS via service role (project_board_versions_insert_trigger
163:    // has WITH CHECK false, so user-scoped client cannot INSERT directly).
164:    const svc = createSupabaseService();
165:    // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
166:    await (svc as any).from("project_board_versions").insert({
167:      board_id: board.id,
168:      version: nextVersion,
169:      document: parsed.data.document,
170:      created_by: user.id,
171:      label: null,
172:    });
173:  }
175:  revalidatePath(`/[locale]/app/projects/${parsed.data.projectId}`, "page");
176:  return { ok: true, boardId: board.id };
177:}

234:export async function toggleBoardLockAction(
235:  boardId: string,
236:  locked: boolean
237:): Promise<ToggleBoardLockResult> {
238:  if (!boardId || typeof boardId !== "string") {
239:    return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
240:  }
241:  if (typeof locked !== "boolean") {
242:    return { ok: false, error: "validation" };
243:  }
245:  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
246:  const {
247:    data: { user },
248:  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
249:  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };
251:  // Action-layer role check (defense-in-depth over RPC-only check)
252:  const { data: roles } = await supabase
253:    .from("user_roles")
254:    .select("role")
255:    .eq("user_id", user.id);
256:  const isYagiAdmin = (roles ?? []).some(
257:    (r) => (r as { role: string }).role === "yagi_admin"
258:  );
259:  if (!isYagiAdmin) return { ok: false, error: "forbidden" };
261:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1: RPC not in generated types
262:  const { error } = await (supabase as any).rpc("toggle_project_board_lock", {
263:    p_board_id: boardId,
264:    p_locked: locked,
265:  });
266:  if (error) {
267:    console.error("[toggleBoardLockAction] rpc error:", error);
268:    return { ok: false, error: "db", message: error.message };
269:  }
271:  // Resolve project_id for revalidation
272:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
273:  const { data: boardLookup } = await (supabase as any)

276:    .eq("id", boardId)
277:    .maybeSingle();
279:  if (boardLookup?.project_id) {
280:    revalidatePath(
281:      `/[locale]/app/projects/${boardLookup.project_id}`,
282:      "page"
283:    );
284:  }
286:  return { ok: true, isLocked: locked };
287:}

445:// addPdfAttachmentAction
446:// ============================================================
448:export type AddPdfResult =
449:  | { ok: true; attachmentId: string }
450:  | { ok: false; error: string };
452:export async function addPdfAttachmentAction(
453:  boardId: string,
454:  file: File
455:): Promise<AddPdfResult> {
456:  if (!boardId || typeof boardId !== "string") {
457:    return { ok: false, error: "invalid_board_id" };
458:  }
460:  // Validate file
461:  if (file.type !== "application/pdf") {
462:    return { ok: false, error: "not_pdf" };
463:  }
464:  if (file.size > 20 * 1024 * 1024) {
465:    return { ok: false, error: "file_too_large" };
466:  }
467:  if (file.name.length > 200) {
468:    return { ok: false, error: "filename_too_long" };
469:  }
471:  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
472:  const {
473:    data: { user },
474:  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
475:  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };
477:  // Upload to R2 first (server-generated key for this board)
478:  const ext = "pdf";
479:  const uuid = crypto.randomUUID();
480:  const storageKey = `project-board/${boardId}/${uuid}.${ext}`;
482:  try {
483:    const putUrl = await createBriefAssetPutUrl(storageKey, file.type, 600);
484:    const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
485:    const putResp = await fetch(putUrl, {
486:      method: "PUT",
487:      body: arrayBuffer,
488:      headers: { "Content-Type": file.type },
489:    });
490:    if (!putResp.ok) {
491:      return { ok: false, error: "r2_put_failed" };
492:    }
493:  } catch (err) {
494:    console.error("[addPdfAttachmentAction] R2 upload error:", err);
495:    return { ok: false, error: "r2_upload_error" };
496:  }
498:  // Call add_project_board_pdf RPC
499:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1: RPC not in generated types
500:  const { data: attachmentId, error: rpcErr } = await (supabase as any).rpc(
501:    "add_project_board_pdf",
502:    {
503:      p_board_id: boardId,
504:      p_storage_key: storageKey,
505:      p_filename: file.name,
506:      p_size_bytes: file.size,
507:    }
508:  );
509:  if (rpcErr) {
510:    console.error("[addPdfAttachmentAction] RPC error:", rpcErr);
511:    return { ok: false, error: rpcErr.message };
512:  }
514:  // Recompute asset_index server-side (trust boundary L-041)
515:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
516:  await recomputeAndUpdateAssetIndex(supabase as any, boardId);
518:  return { ok: true, attachmentId: attachmentId as string };
519:}

570:): Promise<AddUrlResult> {
571:  if (!boardId) return { ok: false, error: "invalid_board_id" };
573:  // Server-side URL validation (L-042 — only http/https)
574:  if (!validateUrlScheme(url)) {
575:    return { ok: false, error: "invalid_url_scheme" };
576:  }
577:  if (url.length > 2000) return { ok: false, error: "url_too_long" };
578:  if (note && note.length > 500) return { ok: false, error: "note_too_long" };
580:  const supabase = await createSupabaseServer();
581:  const {
582:    data: { user },
583:  } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
584:  if (!user) return { ok: false, error: "unauthenticated" };
586:  // Detect provider and fetch metadata
587:  let provider: "youtube" | "vimeo" | "generic" = "generic";
588:  let title: string | null = null;
589:  let thumbnail_url: string | null = null;
591:  try {
592:    const parsedUrl = new URL(url);
593:    const host = parsedUrl.hostname.replace(/^www\./, "");
594:    if (host === "youtube.com" || host === "youtu.be") provider = "youtube";
595:    else if (host === "vimeo.com") provider = "vimeo";
596:    else title = host;
597:  } catch {
598:    // ignore parse error — URL already validated above
599:  }
601:  if (provider !== "generic") {
602:    try {
603:      const meta = await fetchVideoMetadata(url);
604:      if (meta) {
605:        title = meta.title ?? null;
606:        thumbnail_url = meta.thumbnailUrl ?? null;
607:      }
608:    } catch {
609:      // best-effort — fall back to no metadata
610:    }
611:  }
613:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1: RPC not in generated types
614:  const { data: attachmentId, error: rpcErr } = await (supabase as any).rpc(
615:    "add_project_board_url",
616:    {
617:      p_board_id: boardId,
618:      p_url: url,
619:      p_title: title,
620:      p_thumbnail_url: thumbnail_url,
621:      p_provider: provider,
622:      p_note: note,
623:    }
624:  );
625:  if (rpcErr) {
626:    console.error("[addUrlAttachmentAction] RPC error:", rpcErr);
627:    return { ok: false, error: rpcErr.message };
628:  }
630:  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any -- Phase 3.1 tables not in generated types
631:  await recomputeAndUpdateAssetIndex(supabase as any, boardId);
632:  return { ok: true, attachmentId: attachmentId as string };
633:}

CREATE POLICY project_boards_update_client ON project_boards
  FOR UPDATE
  USING (
    is_yagi_admin(auth.uid())
    OR (
      is_locked = false
      AND project_id IN (
        SELECT p.id FROM projects p
        WHERE p.workspace_id IN (
          SELECT workspace_id FROM workspace_members WHERE user_id = auth.uid()
        )
      )
    )
  )
  WITH CHECK (
    is_yagi_admin(auth.uid())

      is_locked = false

        SELECT p.id FROM projects p
        WHERE p.workspace_id IN (
          SELECT workspace_id FROM workspace_members WHERE user_id = auth.uid()
        )
      )
    )
  );

"use client";

/**
 * brief-board-attachments-client.tsx
 * Phase 3.1 hotfix-3 ??Client wrapper that wires server-action callbacks
 * to <AttachmentsSection> in brief mode (project detail page).
 *
 * Why a wrapper?
 *   - page.tsx is a Server Component and cannot pass server actions directly
 *     as props to "use client" children. Instead, the server component renders
 *     this wrapper with boardId + initial data, and this wrapper calls the
 *     server actions via their imported references (which Next.js serialises
 *     as RPC stubs on the client).
 *   - AttachmentsSection performs optimistic state updates internally, but
 *     actual persistence is delegated to the server actions here.
 *
 * L-033: Canvas-internal PDF/URL drop is separate (handled in project-board.tsx).
 *         This section is for explicit attachment management below the canvas.
 * L-041: Trust boundary enforced server-side in each action ??client never
 *         supplies asset_index.
 */

import { useState, useCallback } from "react";
import { AttachmentsSection } from "./attachments-section";
import {
  addPdfAttachmentAction,
  removePdfAttachmentAction,
  addUrlAttachmentAction,
  updateUrlNoteAction,
  removeUrlAttachmentAction,
} from "@/app/[locale]/app/projects/[id]/board-actions";
import type { PdfAttachment, UrlAttachment } from "@/lib/board/asset-index";

// ============================================================
// Props
// ============================================================

interface BriefBoardAttachmentsClientProps {
  boardId: string;
  initialPdfs: PdfAttachment[];
  initialUrls: UrlAttachment[];
  isLocked: boolean;
  isReadOnly: boolean;
}

// ============================================================
// Component
// ============================================================

export function BriefBoardAttachmentsClient({
  boardId,
  initialPdfs,
  initialUrls,
  isLocked,
  isReadOnly,
}: BriefBoardAttachmentsClientProps) {
  // Local optimistic state ??server is source of truth but we update locally
  // so the UI feels responsive without waiting for server round-trip.
  const [pdfs, setPdfs] = useState<PdfAttachment[]>(initialPdfs);
  const [urls, setUrls] = useState<UrlAttachment[]>(initialUrls);

  // ============================================================
  // PDF handlers
  // ============================================================

  const handlePdfAdd = useCallback(
    async (file: File): Promise<void> => {
      // Optimistic: add a placeholder entry while uploading
      const tempId = `temp-${crypto.randomUUID()}`;
      const optimistic: PdfAttachment = {
        id: tempId,
        storage_key: "",
        filename: file.name,
        size_bytes: file.size,
        uploaded_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        uploaded_by: "",
      };
      setPdfs((prev) => [...prev, optimistic]);

      const result = await addPdfAttachmentAction(boardId, file);
      if (result.ok) {
        // Replace temp entry with real entry (real id from RPC)
        setPdfs((prev) =>
          prev.map((p) =>
            p.id === tempId ? { ...optimistic, id: result.attachmentId } : p
          )
        );
      } else {
        // Roll back optimistic update
        setPdfs((prev) => prev.filter((p) => p.id !== tempId));
        throw new Error(result.error);
      }
    },
    [boardId]
  );

  const handlePdfRemove = useCallback(
    async (id: string): Promise<void> => {
      // Optimistic: remove immediately
      setPdfs((prev) => prev.filter((p) => p.id !== id));

      const result = await removePdfAttachmentAction(boardId, id);
      if (!result.ok) {
        // Server failed ??we cannot easily restore the item without re-fetching.
        // Log and surface via console; full refresh will correct state.
        console.error("[BriefBoardAttachmentsClient] PDF remove failed:", result.error);
      }
    },
    [boardId]
  );

  // ============================================================
  // URL handlers
  // ============================================================

  const handleUrlAdd = useCallback(
    async (url: string, note: string | null): Promise<void> => {
      const tempId = `temp-${crypto.randomUUID()}`;
      const optimistic: UrlAttachment = {
        id: tempId,
        url,
        title: null,
        thumbnail_url: null,
        provider: "generic",
        note: note,
        added_at: new Date().toISOString(),
        added_by: "",
      };
      setUrls((prev) => [...prev, optimistic]);

      const result = await addUrlAttachmentAction(boardId, url, note);
      if (result.ok) {
        setUrls((prev) =>
          prev.map((u) =>
            u.id === tempId ? { ...optimistic, id: result.attachmentId } : u
          )
        );
      } else {
        setUrls((prev) => prev.filter((u) => u.id !== tempId));
        throw new Error(result.error);
      }
    },
    [boardId]
  );

  const handleUrlNoteUpdate = useCallback(
    async (id: string, note: string): Promise<void> => {
      // Optimistic update
      setUrls((prev) =>
        prev.map((u) => (u.id === id ? { ...u, note } : u))
      );

      const result = await updateUrlNoteAction(boardId, id, note);
      if (!result.ok) {
        console.error("[BriefBoardAttachmentsClient] URL note update failed:", result.error);
      }
    },
    [boardId]
  );

  const handleUrlRemove = useCallback(
    async (id: string): Promise<void> => {
      setUrls((prev) => prev.filter((u) => u.id !== id));

      const result = await removeUrlAttachmentAction(boardId, id);
      if (!result.ok) {
        console.error("[BriefBoardAttachmentsClient] URL remove failed:", result.error);
      }
    },
    [boardId]
  );

  // ============================================================
  // Render
  // ============================================================

  return (
    <AttachmentsSection
      mode="brief"
      boardId={boardId}
      pdfs={pdfs}
      urls={urls}
      onPdfAdd={handlePdfAdd}
      onPdfRemove={handlePdfRemove}
      onUrlAdd={handleUrlAdd}
      onUrlNoteUpdate={handleUrlNoteUpdate}
      onUrlRemove={handleUrlRemove}
      isLocked={isLocked}
      isReadOnly={isReadOnly}
    />
  );
}

- Severity: HIGH-A  
  Location: `supabase/migrations/20260429144523_phase_3_1_hotfix_3_attachments.sql:350`  
  Description: The new defaulted `seed_project_board_from_wizard(uuid,jsonb,jsonb,jsonb,jsonb)` overload reintroduces a callable 2/4/5-arg SECURITY DEFINER seed path without the pr
ior `auth.uid()` and `projects.created_by` ownership gate. It also accepts caller-supplied `attached_pdfs`, `attached_urls`, and `asset_index` directly. A direct RPC caller can see
d or overwrite any `in_review` project board and inject arbitrary attachment/index JSON.  
  Recommendation: Re-add the K-05 auth gate to this overload, require `projects.created_by = auth.uid()` or explicit admin policy, validate attachment JSON shape/content, remove or
 strictly protect caller-supplied `asset_index`, and `REVOKE ALL`/`GRANT EXECUTE` explicitly for the new signature.

- Severity: HIGH-A  
  Location: `supabase/migrations/20260429113853_phase_3_1_project_board.sql:60` and `supabase/migrations/20260429144523_phase_3_1_hotfix_3_attachments.sql:8`  
  Description: The new `attached_pdfs`, `attached_urls`, and existing `asset_index` columns inherit the broad `project_boards_update_client` policy. Authenticated workspace members
 can bypass the attachment RPCs and directly update these JSON columns, bypassing URL/storage-key validation, count/size limits, server-side asset-index recomputation, and attachme
nt ID generation.  
  Recommendation: Do not expose direct table updates for these columns. Revoke direct `UPDATE` where applicable, split policies/functions so board document writes and attachment wr
ites go through validated RPCs, and keep `asset_index` writable only by trusted server/service code.

- Severity: HIGH-B  
  Location: `supabase/migrations/20260429144523_phase_3_1_hotfix_3_attachments.sql:52`  
  Description: All four attachment RPCs check `projects.owner_id`, but this schema uses `projects.created_by`; no `projects.owner_id` column exists. This breaks the owner authoriza
tion path and will error when the RPC executes.  
  Recommendation: Replace `p.owner_id = v_caller_id` with `p.created_by = v_caller_id` in all four RPCs.

- Severity: MEDIUM  
  Location: `supabase/migrations/20260429144523_phase_3_1_hotfix_3_attachments.sql:80`  
  Description: PDF `p_storage_key` validation accepts any `project-board/%` and any `project-wizard/%`; it does not require `project-board/<p_board_id>/...` or bind wizard assets t
o the caller/project. A direct RPC caller who knows another object key can attach it to their board.  
  Recommendation: Require `p_storage_key LIKE ('project-board/' || p_board_id::text || '/%')` for board uploads, or validate a caller-owned wizard namespace. Also reject null bytes
, backslashes, `//`, and non-positive sizes.

- Severity: MEDIUM  
  Location: `src/app/[locale]/app/projects/[id]/board-actions.ts:477`  
  Description: `addPdfAttachmentAction` uploads to R2 before the RPC performs board ownership and lock checks. Unauthorized or locked-board calls can still create orphaned R2 objec
ts under attacker-supplied `boardId` paths.  
  Recommendation: Preflight board ownership and lock state before creating/uploading the object, and delete the object if the DB RPC fails.

- Severity: MEDIUM  
  Location: `supabase/migrations/20260429144523_phase_3_1_hotfix_3_attachments.sql:39`  
  Description: The RPCs read `is_locked` and counts, then perform a later unguarded `UPDATE`. A concurrent admin lock between read and update can still allow a non-admin mutation; 
concurrent adds can also exceed count caps.  
  Recommendation: Use `SELECT ... FOR UPDATE` on the board row or make the final `UPDATE` conditional on the current lock/count state.

Overall verdict: `LOOP_1_FAIL` because HIGH-A issues are present.
